### `spoof-era-fidelity-18-not-17` — era-real, confidence medium (finder: cadence-spoof-coupling)

**Mechanism:** Q3: the spoof makes a modern client behave cadence-identically to an ERA client for the untouchable client-side mechanics — era clients had no charge meter and ran the ×0.6 self-slow + un-sprint unconditionally per bonus click (SYNOPSIS.md:138); at attack_speed=1024 the delay is ~0.02 ticks so scale=1.0 on every click, even same-tick re-clicks and post-miss ticker resets (attackStrengthTicker=0 → (0+0.5)/0.0195 clamps to 1.0), so the gated branch fires at era frequency. But the result is a 1.8.9-shaped client, not 1.7.10: (1) the client-hardcoded miss penalty survives — a whiffed click sets missTime=10 (survival) and swallows clicks inside the client (SYNOPSIS.md:372-378); 1.8.9 had the same lockout, 1.7.10 swung free — the spoof neutralizes only the charge-reset half of the whiff cost, not the lockout; close-range whiffs still eat clicks the server never sees. (2) The local prediction of the VICTIM-copy knock uses modern knockback() math (m/2 compounding, 0.7h — SYNOPSIS.md:347-349), not legacy addVelocity 0.9h — visual-only, corrected by Mental's authoritative velocity packet. (3) Client crit/sweep gates open at full charge — sweep re-suppressed server-side by B5(d) (AttackCooldownUnit.java:76-91; documented no-op below 1.11), crits add zero KB. The un-sprint/self-slow contract itself is faithfully restored.

**Trigger:** attack-cooldown ON, modern client: every bonus click self-slows and un-sprints (era cadence); whiffed clicks at close range still cost a 10-tick client lockout (1.8.9-authentic, 1.7.10-divergent) — a spam trader's 'hits that never happened' remain possible on the client side and are outside Mental's reach.

**Evidence:** CooldownSpoof.java:23-25 (stated era intent: 'restores that feel'), :37-43 (1024 ceiling, delay math); SYNOPSIS.md:138 (1.7.10 unconditional prediction), :354 (ticker resets on attack/swap/miss — all neutralized by the tiny delay), :372-378 (missTime=10 kept and sharpened; continueAttack clears on release); legacy-combat.md:88-93 (miss penalty is client-side, Mental neutralizes only the damage side), :102-104 (attack indicator can't be hidden); AttackCooldownUnit.java:40-44,76-91 (sweep re-disable rationale + sub-1.11 no-op).

**Maps to the report:** Weakly — spoofed deployments restore era 0.6^n (covered in the dichotomy finding); the residual 1.8.9 miss lockout can eat close-range clicks that the player perceives as landed-but-no-knockback, but that is client-authentic on 1.8.9 too and independent of Mental.

**CODE lens: STANDS** — era call: `era-real`

- Reasoning: I read CooldownSpoof.java, AttackCooldownUnit.java, and the cited SYNOPSIS/legacy-combat sections. Every technical claim in the finding is backed by the code:

(a) Spoof sets attack_speed=1024 (CooldownSpoof.java:43), cooldownPeriod=20/1024 ~=0.0195; with vanilla's +0.5 half-tick adjust, (0+0.5)/0.0195 ~=25 clamps to 1.0 on every click, even post-miss ticker resets. The gated branches (self-slow x0.6, un-sprint) therefore fire every click = era cadence. Correct.
(1) Miss-lockout survives: SYNOPSIS.md:372-378 shows missTime=10 kept on modern/1.8.9 clients; 1.7.10 swung free (legacy-combat.md:88). Spoof neutralizes only the charge-reset (damage) half, not the client lockout. Correct and explicitly documented as unmirrorable.
(2) Victim-copy prediction uses modern knockback() m/2 compounding 0.7h vs legacy addVelocity 0.9h (SYNOPSIS.md:347-349,382), visual-only, overwritten by Mental's authoritative velocity packet. Correct.
(3) Sweep re-suppressed server-side by B5(d), documented no-op below 1.11 (AttackCooldownUnit.java:76-91); crits add zero KB in all eras. Correct.

I cannot refute the core mechanism; it is a faithful reading of the code and era sources. This is not a Mental code defect but confirmation that the residual is a real client behavior outside any server plugin's reach, as legacy-combat.md documents under 'What a server cannot mirror.'

Relevance caveat (finding self-admits 'matches_report: Weakly'): the miss-lockout produces SWALLOWED clicks (no hit, no damage, no KB), not a LANDED hit with weak KB. The user's core symptom is 'the victim doesn't really move back' on a hit that connects, so this residual does NOT explain that symptom; at most it adds a diffuse close-range 'fewer hits register' feel. Technically sound but tangential to the reported weak-KB-on-landed-hits pathway.
- Corrections: Finding stands: all code/era claims verified against CooldownSpoof.java:43, AttackCooldownUnit.java:76-91, SYNOPSIS.md:138/347-349/372-378/382, legacy-combat.md:88-104. The spoof correctly restores era-cadence firing of the untouchable client contracts (x0.6 self-slow + un-sprint per full-charge click), and the residual 1.8.9 miss-lockout is genuinely client-side and outside Mental's reach, not a plugin defect. era_call=era-real: the residual is authentic to real 1.8.9 clients and legacy-combat.md already documents it as unmirrorable. (Nuance: measured against Mental's stated 1.7.10 combat-model target the lockout is a per-era divergence, but since it is purely client-side and Mental introduces nothing, 'era-real / not-a-bug / unfixable' is the honest call.) IMPORTANT relevance correction: this residual causes SWALLOWED clicks (no hit at all), not landed hits with weak knockback, so it does NOT explain the user's 'victim doesn't really move back on a hit that connects' symptom. It is at most a minor diffuse contributor to a close-range feel and should not be treated as the report's root pathway (which is the sprint/w-tap KB-scaling side covered by other findings).
- Severity: low

**SYMPTOM lens: STANDS** — era call: `era-real`

- Reasoning: Mechanism confirmed: CooldownSpoof rewrites attack_speed to 1024 so client scale=1.0 every click, restoring era cadence for the untouchable client mechanics (self-slow ×0.6, un-sprint). SYNOPSIS.md:372-378 confirms the surviving 1.8.9 miss penalty: MISS sets missTime=10, swallowing clicks inside the client for ~10 ticks; the spoof only neutralizes the charge-reset half, never the lockout. This IS 1.8.9-authentic and outside Mental's reach.\n\nSymptom-shape test: the report describes hits that LAND but carry weak/non-sprint knockback (victim takes the hit but doesn't fly back). The miss-lockout produces the opposite shape — swallowed clicks mean NO attack packet, NO hit, NO damage, NO knockback at all. During a close-range spam exchange a trader could loosely perceive this as 'my hits aren't connecting,' so it weakly touches the report's 'subtle feeling' and close-range emphasis. But it cannot produce the central symptom (landed hits with non-sprint KB) — that is the sprint-flag/self-slow dichotomy the finding itself defers to another finding.\n\nAttribution: fires only with the default-OFF ATTACK_COOLDOWN feature enabled, and even then it is client-authentic 1.8.9 behavior identical to what the owner would see on any modern/1.8.9 client — not a Mental defect. Not refuted (weak fringe contribution to the 'hits that never happened' feeling), but wrong symptom shape for the core complaint and low severity.
- Corrections: The surviving client miss-penalty (missTime=10 lockout, SYNOPSIS.md:372-378) is a genuine but weak contributor to the report. It only manifests when the default-OFF ATTACK_COOLDOWN feature is enabled, and even then it is faithful 1.8.9 client behavior that Mental cannot touch (independent of the plugin). Crucially it produces the WRONG symptom shape: it swallows close-range spam clicks so the attack packet is never sent — yielding no hit, no damage, and no knockback at all — rather than the report's described 'landed hit that carries non-sprinting knockback.' The core symptom (weak/non-sprint KB on hits that visibly register) is the sprint-flag / self-slow pathway, not this. So this finding is at most a fringe amplifier of the 'hits that never happened / feeling' portion at close range during spam, and is not a Mental bug to fix.
- Severity: low

### `spoof-listener-folia-entityid-throw` — bug, confidence medium (finder: cadence-spoof-coupling)

**Mechanism:** CooldownSpoofListener.onPacketSend runs on the netty thread and calls receiver.getEntityId() inside its try block (CooldownSpoofListener.java:41). The netty-fast-path skill's measured Folia probe lists entity.getEntityId() as a THROWER off the owning region ('any getHandle()-routed accessor' — IllegalStateException), and the catch(Exception ignored) at :47-49 swallows it — on Folia the client-presentation half (mandate B5(b): 'no charge overlay even on the first sync') silently no-ops for every outbound UPDATE_ATTRIBUTES. Masking: the server attribute base IS 1024 (AttackChargeReset), so genuine attribute syncs already carry the spoofed value and the injection path only matters for batches omitting attack_speed after the client already holds 1024 — practical impact near zero, but the packet half violates its own stated contract on Folia and the failure is invisible (swallowed per-packet). Same-family precedent: the 2.0.x netty getEntityId regression documented in the skill.

**Trigger:** Folia server + ATTACK_COOLDOWN ON: every UPDATE_ATTRIBUTES parse attempt throws at receiver.getEntityId() and is swallowed; the rewrite/inject never runs. Observable only in the corner where a client would need the injected property (e.g. a third-party plugin sending a custom attribute batch with attack_speed 4.0 — that batch ships unspoofed).

**Evidence:** CooldownSpoofListener.java:36-49 (getEntityId inside try on the netty thread; blanket catch); .claude/skills/netty-fast-path/SKILL.md:26-34 (measured Folia probe: entity.getEntityId() THROWS from a netty-like thread; the catch-all-eats-the-feature failure family); AttackChargeReset.java:85-98 (the masking server-side base raise).

**Maps to the report:** No — cosmetic/contract issue only, no knockback effect; reported for axis completeness.

**CODE lens: STANDS** — era call: `bug`

- Reasoning: Confirmed via javap on the actual server jars (nms-archaeology). Real Folia 1.21.11 CraftEntity.getHandle() calls ca/spottedleaf/moonrise/.../TickThread.ensureTickThread("Accessing entity state off owning region's thread") and getEntityId()=getHandle().getId(), so receiver.getEntityId() at CooldownSpoofListener.java:41 THROWS on the netty thread (never a region thread) on Folia; the catch(Exception ignored) at :47-49 swallows it, so the client-presentation half no-ops for every outbound UPDATE_ATTRIBUTES. Real Paper 1.21.11 getHandle() is a bare field return (no ensureTickThread) — so the defect is Folia-ONLY, exactly as the finding states. The rim (PacketTap/ValveListener/etc.) uniformly resolves identity via event.getUser() (PacketEvents cached User, no getHandle) — the established Folia-safe idiom that this listener deviates from; the fix is event.getUser().getEntityId(). Mechanism is not refutable. Severity is very low: (1) Folia-only; (2) ATTACK_COOLDOWN is default-OFF; (3) near-zero practical impact — AttackChargeReset already raises the server attack_speed base to 1024, so genuine UPDATE_ATTRIBUTES already carry 1024 and the listener's rewrite is itself a no-op (CooldownSpoof:62-63) for those; only exotic corners (a plugin sending a non-1024 attack_speed batch, or omitting it) need the rewrite/inject; (4) zero knockback effect — does NOT explain the user's weak-close-range-KB report. era_call=bug: a genuine swallowed-throw code defect, unrelated to era authenticity, gated behind Folia + feature-on.
- Corrections: Mechanism CONFIRMED against the shipping Folia jar, not refutable. javap on run/folia-1.21.11/.../folia-1.21.11.jar: CraftEntity.getHandle() invokes TickThread.ensureTickThread(entity,"Accessing entity state off owning region's thread"); getEntityId()=getHandle().getId(). CraftPlayer inherits it. So receiver.getEntityId() (CooldownSpoofListener.java:41) throws IllegalStateException on the netty thread on Folia, caught+swallowed at :47, so CooldownSpoofListener no-ops for every outbound UPDATE_ATTRIBUTES on Folia. Verified Folia-ONLY: Paper 1.21.11 getHandle() is a bare field return with no ensureTickThread. Corroborating: the rim (PacketTap/ValveListener/ProbeRim/TransactionProbeRim) all use event.getUser() (PacketEvents cached User) — never event.getPlayer() — the established Folia-safe identity idiom; the one-line fix is to compare packet.getEntityId() against event.getUser().getEntityId(). Severity remains very low and the finding's own scoping is accurate: Folia-only, ATTACK_COOLDOWN default-OFF, and near-zero practical impact (AttackChargeReset already sets the server base to 1024, so real syncs carry 1024 and the listener rewrite is itself a no-op for them; only rare custom/omitting attribute batches are affected). Crucially matches_report=No is correct — this is cosmetic, has ZERO knockback effect, and does not explain the user's weak-close-range-KB report. Report it only as a Folia contract-hygiene fix, not as a lead on the bug.
- Severity: low

**SYMPTOM lens: REFUTED** — era call: `bug`

- Reasoning: Verified CooldownSpoofListener.java:36-49 and CooldownSpoof.java. The listener mutates ONLY the packet-local attack_speed property in outbound UPDATE_ATTRIBUTES — a purely CLIENT-presentation value (client computes the swing-cooldown overlay as delay=(1/attack_speed)*20; at 1024 the bar never shows). It writes nothing to the velocity path. Knockback ships through DeliveryDesk/MotionLedger/PlayerVelocityEvent, which never reads attack_speed. The finding's own matches_report says "No — cosmetic/contract issue only, no knockback effect." I confirm: hand-computing shipped velocity with vs without the injection yields IDENTICAL velocity in every case — the injection touches zero terms of the knockback equation (base, friction, sprint bonus, residual). The line-41 getEntityId() throw-and-swallow IS a real Folia defect (matches the skill's measured probe: any getHandle()-routed accessor throws off-region, catch(Exception ignored) eats it), but: (1) Folia-only, (2) CADENCE/ATTACK_COOLDOWN family is default-OFF, (3) even when it no-ops the only visible effect is a cosmetic charge bar on a first sync in a corner case, and the functional half (server base=1024 via AttackChargeReset) still works regardless. It cannot produce "little to no knockback," cannot weaken sprint hits, and has no close-range dependence. Refuted for the symptom; the underlying cosmetic bug is real but out of scope.
- Corrections: The finding describes a genuine but cosmetic Folia defect: CooldownSpoofListener.onPacketSend calls receiver.getEntityId() on the netty thread (CooldownSpoofListener.java:41), which the skill's measured Folia probe lists as a THROWER off the owning region; the blanket catch(Exception ignored) at 47-49 swallows it, so the attack_speed spoof silently no-ops for outbound UPDATE_ATTRIBUTES on Folia. This is real and worth fixing (cache the entityId at scope-open, or gate the packet-half comparison on a pre-resolved id) but it is NOT a cause of the weak-knockback report. The spoofed attribute is CLIENT-presentation only (charge-bar rendering); the functional cooldown removal is the server-side base=1024 set by AttackChargeReset, unaffected by the throw. No term of the knockback equation reads attack_speed, so shipped velocity is byte-identical with or without the injection. The symptom is not explained by this pathway.
- Severity: low


---

# FINAL SYNTHESIS — ranked diagnosis (2026-07-09)

Three rounds, 13 finder agents, ~120 raw findings, every surviving finding attacked by two
independent Opus lenses. The report — "some hits have little to no knockback, especially in
close trades; sprint/w-tap/blockhit hits feel non-sprint; subtle, can't pin it down" — is a
**stack**, not one bug. Partitioned by what the evidence supports:

## Tier 1 — Confirmed default-config bugs (fix candidates, in recommended order)

1. **`same-tick-wtap-start-retro-clear`** (both lenses, round 1). A genuine w-tap whose
   START_SPRINTING arrives in the same tick as the ATTACK is retroactively destroyed:
   `onServerClear(asOf = verdict stamp)` drops wire sprinting+armed unless `lastWrite` is
   *strictly newer* than the stamp (SprintWire.java:103) — same-tick writes lose. The very
   next hit reads a plain verdict. Matches "even if one is w-tapping, it feels non-sprint"
   verbatim. Fix direction: arrival-order sequence (the wire already observes program order
   on the netty thread) instead of tick-granularity stamps, so a START that arrived after
   the ATTACK survives the clear that belongs to that ATTACK.

2. **`presend-marked-before-ship-outcome-discarded-valve-eats-only-copy`** (code lens
   verified the full chain, round 3). `HitRegistrationUnit.plan()` commits `tx.preSent()`
   at :409 *before* `senders.ship()` at :427 and discards the ship `Outcome`;
   `BurstSender.ship()` catches all Throwables/null-user and returns UNSENDABLE having sent
   nothing; the phantom PRE_SENT still resolves SHIP_AND_ARM_VALVE and the valve cancels the
   authoritative ENTITY_VELOCITY. **Zero velocity packets reach the client while damage and
   flinch land; the journal records a healthy ship.** Rare per hit (1.20.2+ reconfigure
   mid-combat, transient encode throw, user-null race) — a memorable total-zero-KB hit.
   Fix: capture the Outcome; on UNSENDABLE pin instead of preSent (the BurstSender javadoc
   :22-23 already states this contract; only the plan-time null check honors it).

3. **`valve-arm-lifecycle-races`** (both lenses, round 3). Two code-valid legs:
   (a) a HIGHEST/MONITOR third-party listener cancelling/modifying PlayerVelocityEvent after
   DeskRouter (HIGH, no isCancelled check) leaves a dead arm keyed only by
   (recipient, entityId, 3 quantized shorts) — stationary close trades produce byte-identical
   stamps, so the *next* hit's pre-send burst is consumed against the dead arm and that hit
   reaches the client with zero velocity copies; cascades across an exchange. Needs a foreign
   velocity-touching plugin (anticheat/anti-KB) — realistic.
   (b) blocked-redelivery (ordinary shield/temp-shield block-hits, always-on path via
   `freshBlockedKnock`) arms in the TASK phase but its duplicate only emits at the end-of-tick
   tracker, breaking arm→dup adjacency; the unconditional per-session-tick `clearStale`
   (SessionService:348, no age check) can fire between them. Fix direction: hit-identity or
   generation in the valve key, age-aware clearStale, disarm on observed event cancellation.

4. **`desk-single-slot-supersede-passthrough-vanilla-leak`** (sym: bug; code: config-dependent,
   round 1). The desk's one-slot wire inbox: a superseding second hit resets the first to
   not-awaiting, which resolves PASS_THROUGH — vanilla's damage-pass velocity stands, which is
   **base-only 0.4 with no sprint/enchant extras** (Player.attack never ran). A weak,
   non-sprint-feeling hit under fast-trade conditions. Fix: a superseded pending must be
   delivered or cancelled, never passed through.

5. **`presend-enchant-extra-dropped`** / **`presend-attacker-enchant-level-zero-adopted`**
   (independently found rounds 2+3, all four lenses stand). The pre-send builds the attacker
   state with `knockbackEnchantLevel = 0` (netty can't read inventory; comment claims "corrected
   on the authoritative pass") but PRE_SENT/PINNED vectors are adopted verbatim — the correction
   never happens; region-path hits read the live item and ship FULL, so KB-sword knockback
   alternates weak/full by path. A non-sprint KB-enchant hit ships 0.4h where era ships 0.9h.
   Off-axis for the owner's own report unless KB swords are in play, but a confirmed contract
   violation. Fix: freeze the enchant level into the per-tick PlayerView.

6. **`ring-origin-fallback-first-tick`** (both lenses, round 2) — first-tick ring fallback ships
   a wrong-origin direction; small and transient. **`superseded-upgrade-reverts-owner-edit`**
   (code lens, round 3) — `upgradeSupersededPreset` runs every boot/reload and silently reverts
   any owner edit that lands on a superseded revision; the bundled files' own "Restore -3.9 to
   unfloor" comment instructs exactly such an edit. Violates "owner edits are sacred". Plus the
   three dead latency knobs (`ping-offset-ms`, `spike-threshold-ms`, `off-ground-sync` parsed,
   consumed by nothing) and `spoof-listener-folia-entityid-throw` (Folia-only). Config debt.

## Tier 2 — Divergences from era (default config; make sprint hits plain more often than era)

- **`modern-client-no-reengage-after-clear`**, premise corrected by round 3
  (`no-reengage-premise-corrected-spoof-cures-it`): the modern client still predicts the attack
  sprint-reset in 2026, but only at charge > 0.9 — so at spam CPS an **unspoofed** modern client
  never emits the STOP/START pair, Mental's era-authentic post-hit clear leaves the wire plain,
  and the reconcile only rescues after ~3 ticks: recurring plain-sprint gaps on hits 2..n.
  **Enabling ATTACK_COOLDOWN (the CADENCE spoof, default OFF) cures it** — attack_speed 1024
  pins client charge at 1.0, the prediction fires every click, STOP/START re-arms era-style.
  Also splits populations: Via 1.7/1.8 clients re-arm; modern clients don't — the same trade
  feels different per player.
- **`recompute-extras-ride-damage-time-yaw`** (round 2): suppressed pre-sends (anticheat AUTO,
  pace-outs) recompute with the attacker's yaw 1–2 ticks after the click — extras ship along a
  stale-flick direction.
- **`stale-position-ring-direction-at-close-range`** (refuted in round 1 on strafe magnitudes;
  reinstated in round 3 with the correct displacement source): the attacker's OWN received knock
  moves them 0.4–0.9 b/t — the once-per-tick ring misses up to a tick of that, giving 11–27° of
  base-direction error at ≤1.5 blocks in oblique/circling geometry (5–12% typical along-axis
  loss, 15–30% sub-block; hurt-flinch points wrong too). Head-on trades unaffected.
- `presend-attacker-position-one-tick-stale-vs-era` (round 2): the attacker-side position read
  is categorically one tick staler than era's in-slot live read; the victim-side read matches era.

## Tier 3 — Era-real (authentic feel; do NOT "fix")

- **Mid-invuln economics**: at 10 CPS same-weapon, ~80% of landed clicks legitimately move the
  victim zero (equal/weaker mid-invuln = nothing; stronger = difference damage, no knock).
- **Face-hug opposition**: base pushes from attacker POSITION, sprint extra along attacker YAW —
  measured 0.0546h at 0.14-block separation on real 1.7.10. Degenerate <0.01-block separation
  gets vanilla-equivalent randomized full-magnitude push (not a bug).
- **Client 0.6^clicks self-reduction**: a counter-clicking victim erases their own received
  knockback — fires on Via legacy clients always, on modern clients only with the CADENCE spoof
  ON (or slow full-charge clicking). Era-authentic and untouchable (client prediction).
- **1.7 join-order trade asymmetry** (later-joiner ~0.49 sprint wire; ~0.30 if counter-hitting).
- **Ping-proportional residual lag** (reclassified by round-3 code lens): era 1.7.10 also adopted
  onGround from client packets (compendium §1.6) — Mental is era-faithful; ~2–6% per combo hit
  at 100–150ms, near-nil on ice.
- Post-hit sprint-clear economics; combo residual opposition + liftoff facing push.

## Tier 4 — Config-dependent on THIS server

- **`chase-pocket-sprint-hits-pin-min-clamp-everywhere`** (combo-hold ON — the owner runs the
  Combo Solver): the servo's inverse solve is saturated for sprint-fresh hits across the whole
  2.5–3.5-block chase band → every hit-3+ chase sprint hit ships ×0.93 fresh ≈ **0.29 blocks
  short, deterministically** — and the servo simultaneously misses its own 2.85 pocket target
  (victim lands past it). The 2.4.6 calibration was done at freshEra 0.40 (plain hits) and never
  covered sprint-fresh. Recalibration candidate, owner's call.
- **anticheat.mode AUTO** (default) arms the pre-send suppressor the moment GrimAC/Vulcan is
  present → all hits take the recompute path (stale-yaw extras, Tier 2).
- **SWORD_BLOCKING default OFF** → the block-hit sprint re-arm reconstruction never runs; on era
  clients block-hitting shipped plain DURING the block (era-real) but re-armed on release —
  without the feature the re-arm depends solely on the client's own STOP/START.
- CPS limiter (max-cps 20, hard drop above), legacy-1.8's all-or-nothing resistance roll.

## Default-config gate inventory (round 3, verified)

wtap-registration ON; sword-blocking OFF; combo-hold OFF; combo-reach-handicap OFF; anticheat
AUTO [GrimAC, Vulcan]; max-cps 20; fast-path + pre-send + bundle ON, feedback auto;
reach-validation OFF; default profile legacy-1.7 (combos true, resistance NONE, tracker/tracker,
wtapExtra disabled everywhere, verticalMin 0.0 since 2.4.8); pace scaling signature-only;
armor-resistance LEGACY only on legacy-1.8; all DAMAGE/CADENCE/SUSTAIN/LOADOUT rules OFF.

## The discriminating measurement (before/with any fix)

One per-hit DeliveryDesk-journal capture during a live wired close-range w-tap trade, logging:
verdict.sprinting + verdict.fresh · pre-send disposition (admitted/suppressed-by-what) · resolve
outcome (SHIP_AND_ARM_VALVE / adopt / PASS_THROUGH / CANCEL) · shipped h,v + the ring positions
and attacker yaw fed to base() · effective profile + enabled families. It cleanly separates:
verdict flips false on a real w-tap → Tier-1 #1; flag true but shipped-h low → Tier-3 geometry;
PASS_THROUGH → Tier-1 #4; healthy SHIP but the client never moved → Tier-1 #2/#3.

## Open, deployment-dependent (not code-resolvable from this repo)

ViaVersion transcoding vs the valve byte-match on 1.21.9+ (~32% observed re-quantization
mismatch — usually harmless double-send, harmful only combined with Tier-1 #3); Folia
cross-region trades; chronic low-TPS view staleness (systematic Vanilla-source fallthrough).
